Spanish Confiscation

Catholic Church Library

A Reuters dispatch from Madrid on the 26th reports that the Republican government has ordered the confiscation of a Catholic Church library. This library is located in the Milos Monastery and is one of the world's most famous libraries. This is the first instance of the Spanish government authorities implementing the confiscation of enemy property.

A Reuters dispatch from Madrid on the 26th reports that today's newspapers stated that the Catholic authorities in the provinces of Navarre and Basque are in contact with former bureaucrats and retired military officers at restoration conferences, planning to support the restoration of Alfonso to the throne. The restoration conference was held in Madrid and agreed on restoration emblems for distribution among supporters. However, due to the government's strict precautions, stationing troops at key points and confiscating arsenals, the unrest was nipped in the bud.

Gandhi Decides to Attend

London Round Table Conference

A Reuters dispatch from Simla on the 26th reports that after a three-hour conversation with the Viceroy of India, Gandhi decided today to attend the London Round Table Conference. He is scheduled to depart from Mumbai on a British ship on Saturday or Sunday. He is currently staying in Simla to discuss the wording of the public statement regarding his conversation with the Viceroy. Therefore, he will not be able to arrive in Mumbai until Saturday or Sunday. However, Gandhi's luggage is simple and does not require much time for preparation. Gandhi has not yet notified the British shipping company regarding the type of cabin he intends to book. In India, he usually travels third class. It is rumored that Gandhi will travel to England in steerage, but the shipping company denies this, saying that their ships do not sell steerage tickets except for servants. Furthermore, Malaviya and Mrs. Naidu have also decided to accompany Gandhi to England on Saturday or Sunday.

Important News

Central Executive Committee Resolution

Flood Relief Measures

Transfer Non-Essential Construction Funds for Disaster Relief

Regulations on the Number of Executive and Supervisory Committee Members in the Hunan Provincial Party Headquarters

Dispatch Dai Chuanxian to Guide the Zhejiang Provincial Congress

The Central Executive Committee of the Kuomintang held its 156th Standing Committee meeting at 8:00 AM on the 27th in the first conference hall of the Central Party Headquarters. Attendees included Yu Youren, Ye Chucang, Zhu Peide, and Ding Weifen. Observers included Ding Chaowu, Miao Peicheng, Wu Jingheng, Zhang Daofan, Wang Bailing, Wang Zhengting, Chen Lifu, Shao Yuanchong, Zhu Jiahua, Zeng Yangfu, Yu Jingtang, Chen Bulei, Ke Xing'e, Jiao Yitang, Cai Yuanpei, Fang Juehui, Wang Boqun, and Enke Batu. The meeting was chaired by Ye Chucang. The resolutions are as follows: (1) Regarding the issue of flood relief, the resolution is: (1) The National Government should issue an order to all national institutions to suspend all non-essential construction and transfer the funds to be used for disaster relief. (2) The construction funds of the Central Party Headquarters should be submitted to the Central Government within a limited time. The Central Government will use all of it to purchase flood relief bonds issued by the Ministry of Finance, or lend it to the Ministry of Finance for disaster relief. The uncollected portion of the Central Party Headquarters construction donations will be collected after the flood relief donations have been collected. (3) The National Government should investigate and severely punish officials who are responsible for local and water conservancy affairs who neglect the repair of dikes and the dredging of waterways. (4) The National Government should instruct local officials in each province to be responsible for relocating disaster victims. (5) The National Government should strictly stipulate measures for punishing those who embezzle relief funds, engage in corruption through relief efforts, and are ineffective in handling relief efforts. (6) All party members should do their best to assist the relief personnel dispatched by the government in handling disaster relief. (7) Reduce banquets. (8) Increase taxes on luxury goods. (9) Prohibit the sale and slaughter of draft cattle and properly arrange measures for housing draft cattle. (2) The number of executive and supervisory committee members of the Hunan Provincial Party Headquarters is set at seven executive committee members, five alternate executive committee members, five supervisory committee members, and two alternate supervisory committee members. In accordance with Item C of Article 2 of the Outline of the Provincial Executive and Supervisory Committee Election Law, twice the number of candidates should be elected and submitted to the Central Committee for approval. (3) When the Zhejiang Provincial Congress is convened, send Commissioner Dai Chuanxian to provide guidance. (4) Zhou Dawen will fill the vacancy of Hu Ruoyu, a member of the Party Affairs Reorganization Committee of the Beiping Special City. (5) Wan Dianzun, Xia Yusan, Heng Yunlong, Yang Ting, Ya Ding, Shuheng Feng, Yi Liu, Zizhao and seven others are appointed as preparatory committee members for the Special Party Department of the 8th Division of the Army. (6) Li Yannian, Yuan Jinggu and Lei, three preparatory committee members of the Special Party Department of the Assault Brigade of the Army, Navy and Air Force Headquarters, have resigned successively. Qiu Zhaochen, Hu Qiru and Guo Yulin are appointed to fill the vacancies. (7) The resignation of Fan Qi, director of the Party Ideology Education Section of the Central Training Department, is approved. (8) Zhang Rentian is appointed as the director of the Censorship Section of the Central Propaganda Department. (9) Commissioner Zhu Jiahua is recommended to attend the Central Memorial Week report next week.

Hunan Border

Withdrawal of Guangdong-Guangxi Troops

All Counties in Southern Hunan Report to the Province

A dispatch from Changsha reports that there have been rumors recently that the Guangdong and Guangxi armies are invading Hunan. Until last week, a part of the Guangxi army under Tan Lianfang retreated from the Huangsha River area to Quanzhou. The Guangdong army in Jiufeng Pingshi also withdrew. The Hunan border area has become peaceful. All counties in southern Hunan have sent telegrams reporting: (1) A telegram from Lingling states that according to merchants returning to Hunan from Guangxi, the reason why the Guangxi rebels sent troops across the Hunan border this month was because they heard that the Central Army was preparing to launch a southern expedition, and they had to prepare in advance. Recently, because our army has no troops coming to Yongzhou, the troops crossing the river have retreated to the west bank of the Huangsha River. They have been sending scouts to Guilin and Quanzhou to investigate. The comprehensive situation is as follows: 1. There are about two regiments of rebels in Quanzhou, all of whom are new soldiers. Seventy percent have guns, and the rest are empty-handed. 2. Guilin is currently the concentration point for the rebel armies, and they are rushing to build defenses. It is said that Li (Zongren) and Bai (Chongxi) have also recently arrived there. Because the Shi rebels have been eliminated, the rebels dare not lightly invade. I know the matter is urgent, and I hereby report it. Respectfully, Hu Tianxiang, Magistrate of Lingling County. (2) A telegram from Dong'an states: 1. The Seventh Regiment, Third Battalion, and One Company of the Twenty-fourth Division (Tan Lianfang) formerly stationed in Huangsha River retreated to Quanzhou on the first day of the lunar month. 2. The only military force stationed in Quanzhou is the Quanxing Militia, with mixed guns, mostly made in Han, two machine guns, and a severe shortage of bullets, and two hundred coolies. 3. Quanzhou has been recruiting new soldiers to go to Guilin for several days. 4. Chen En Yuan, the police chief of Quanxingguan, was transferred to Guilin and reorganized into the Fourth Army. 5. Zhang Fakui is still in Hong Kong and has not returned to Guangxi. Respectfully, Li Yaonan, Magistrate of Dong'an County. (3) A telegram from Rucheng states that the Hu Militia Regiment (Hunan) has not returned to defense. The Guangdong army stationed in Jiufeng has withdrawn to Kaitang Village. Only one battalion is stationed in Pingshi, and it also appears to be withdrawing. About two regiments have arrived in Lechang. Remnants of the Guangdong bandits Deng (Shixi) and Yu (Jingbang) have been discovered in Miaotou Xu. Troops have been dispatched to suppress them. Respectfully, Wan Fangzhou, Magistrate of Rucheng County. Secretary Lu Zhengyuan and Deputy Director of the Neighborhood Militia, Hu Fengzhang. (4) A telegram from Qiyang states: 1. According to intelligence reports, about two battalions of rebel troops are stationed in Huangsha River, preparing to return to Quanzhou. The atmosphere of invading Hunan has completely dissipated, and the Yongzhou territory is peaceful. 2. Rumors in subordinate counties have also subsided. Further investigation reports will follow. Respectfully, Yang Yanxuan, Magistrate of Qiyang County. (5) A telegram from Officer Bai states: 1. Guangxi rebel troops in Quanzhou have been withdrawing to Guilin for the past two days. Heavy troops are also stationed in Xing'an, and the situation is serious. 2. It is rumored that Zhang (Fakui)'s troops stationed in Yongwu, because Zhang Fakui himself is in Hong Kong and has not returned, and there is no military pay, the soldiers do not obey orders, and two regiments have rebelled. Li (Zongren) and Bai (Chongxi) and other rebels have transferred troops to prevent disturbances, and the situation is very chaotic. 3. There are no rebel troops in the Huangsha River area. Currently, only the militia is left to defend it. Only one regiment of Tan Lianfang's troops is stationed in Quanzhou. 4. The Guangdong Road Government is controlled by Chen Jitang, the Party power is controlled by Wang (Jingwei), and the military power is controlled by Xiang (Hanping) and Gu (Yingfen). Each has his own plans, and disputes arise from time to time. Financial difficulties and military pay have not been released for several months, and opinions are becoming increasingly chaotic. There is no possibility of invading Hunan. The security of all counties on the Hunan border has returned to normal.

Wang Rongbao Investigates

Report on the Wanxian Incident

After the Wanxian Incident occurred, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs immediately telegraphed Wang Rongbao, the Minister to Japan, to go to investigate. Recently, after Wang returned to China, he reported the facts to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. The full text is as follows:

Confidential report. On July 9th of this year, I received your telegram regarding the Korean incident. The government attaches great importance to it. Please go to investigate and express condolences. After the matter is completed, please come to Beijing, etc. I immediately telegraphed to request a staff member to accompany me and asked Councilor Jiang to temporarily act as the head of the consulate. I also stated that after the matter in Korea is completed, I will go to Liaoning and Yan to investigate and discuss everything, and then return to Beijing immediately. I received a reply telegram approving it. I then scheduled a meeting with Foreign Minister Shidehara and notified him in person. I departed from Tokyo on the 13th of the same month, passing through Kobe. I immediately transferred Consul Ren Jiafeng from the consulate to accompany me and assist in all matters. I went to all the places in Korea where the incidents occurred, including Busan, Seoul, Pyongyang, Zhennampo, Incheon, and Sinuiju. I have telegraphed the general situation in advance. I left Korea on the 23rd, stayed in Andong for one day, and stayed in Shenyang for two days. I met with important local officials and clarified the whole story of the so-called Wanbaoshan Incident. I then took the Beining Line directly to Pingjin, paid my respects to Deputy Commander Zhang, and immediately purchased a boat ticket because I learned that the Jinpu Southern Section was blocked by water. I changed to the sea route and went south, arriving in Shanghai on the 5th of this month and arriving in Beijing today. After investigating the situation in various disaster areas, Pyongyang was the most severely affected, followed by Incheon. The situation in the other areas was relatively early and did not lead to major changes. I will now report the situation in each place separately as follows:

Pyongyang, Zhennampo, On the evening of July 4th, Zhennampo Consul Xu Sui learned that anti-Chinese riots had occurred in Seoul and Incheon. On the morning of the 5th, he formally sent a special telegram to the police chiefs of the South Pyongan and Hwanghae Provincial Governments, the police chief of the Pyongyang Police Station, and personally met with the police chief of the Zhennampo Police Station, entrusting them to protect the overseas Chinese properly. He also discussed preventive measures with the local chamber of commerce. As for the Pyongyang incident, representatives from all walks of life of the local overseas Chinese claimed that at about 11:00 AM on the 5th, they received a phone call from the Pyongyang Police Station, asking the chairman of the chamber of commerce to go to the station for a discussion. At that time, because the chairman had just returned to Andong, the executive committee member Zhang Jingxian and translator Luo went together. They were received by Senior Director Ando, who said that if riots occurred locally, the station would definitely provide effective protection. If Koreans caused trouble, he hoped that they would be particularly tolerant and close their doors early, and they could rest assured. After returning to the chamber of commerce, he immediately notified all overseas Chinese to be cautious and take precautions. By about 7:00 PM, a sudden riot broke out. Countless rioters gathered, holding clubs, knives, axes, stones, and other weapons, and carrying flashlights. They attacked the houses of overseas Chinese, regardless of farmers, industrialists, merchants, and wealthy people, in teams and shifts. They beat our Chinese, regardless of men, women, old, and young, to death. They destroyed and looted property, burned accounts, and carried flammable materials, trying to set fires everywhere. The commanders used police whistles, and the organization was quite complete. It did not stop until dawn. The cruelty was rare in the world. The police at various places did not wear weapons and tried to stop them with their bare hands. What good did that do? By the 9th, it was known that more than a hundred people had been killed, and more than two hundred people had been injured. After investigating the entire Korean anti-Chinese incident, Pyongyang was the most severe. Local government officials did not take serious precautions after receiving telegrams from the consulate. The provincial government had no precautions. The police station made empty promises. After the riots broke out everywhere, they still did not take decisive measures. That night, the police were not armed, and the army did not move out, so the rioters had no fear and were able to carry out their crimes. Their negligence, dereliction of duty, and disregard for the lives and property of our overseas Chinese were such. The Pyongyang overseas Chinese affairs were under the jurisdiction of the Zhennampo Branch. When the branch learned of the matter on the morning of the 6th, there were also unstable rumors in Zhennampo. In addition to discussing emergency measures with the local chamber of commerce and Japanese government officials, Consul Xu Sui took a car directly to Pyongyang. When he arrived at the station, the stationmaster and personnel from the provincial government were waiting to receive him. They said that our overseas Chinese had been properly accommodated, and armed police, troops, and fire brigades had been dispatched. There was nothing to worry about after that. If there was anything to instruct the overseas Chinese and government officials, they would relay the message. It was useless to see them now, and the situation in Zhennampo was very urgent, so please return quickly to take charge. Consul Xu Sui reluctantly agreed to their request and immediately took a car back to Zhennampo. As expected, at about 2:00 PM, Koreans gathered everywhere, and armed police disbanded at any time. Overseas Chinese flocked to the consulate to take refuge. Overseas Chinese in remote farms and shops also negotiated with the police station to send police to search for and escort them. However, those who were a little late had already been beaten. By about 6:00 PM, all were accommodated. At about 7:00 PM, the rioters gathered more and more, and although the police tried to suppress them, they were too few and could not take care of everything. The farms and some shops of our overseas Chinese were still stoned, smashed, looted, and set on fire. On the following 7th, there was even talk of attacking the consulate, because some rioters from Pyongyang came to Pu to help, and the situation became even more dangerous. Fortunately, a telephone was temporarily installed on the evening of the 6th to negotiate directly with the provincial government and send more troops and police, so assistance was provided one after another, and the public was safe. Although property losses were unavoidable, there was no tragedy because of the early accommodation. On the 8th, Consul Xu Sui went to Pyongyang to inspect and express condolences. He also appointed a temporary investigator to investigate the damages in Pyongyang, Zhennampo, and other places together with the investigators from the chamber of commerce. According to the investigation, excluding those who were unable to investigate after returning to China, those who did not report indirect losses, and those who have not yet been recorded, the total losses in Pyongyang are about 2,545,000 yen, and the losses in Zhennampo and other places are about 117,000 yen. As for the number of deaths and injuries in Pyongyang, according to the provincial government, 95 people died. According to our investigation, 109 people died, 163 were injured, and 63 were missing. 19 people were injured in Zhennampo. Rongbao arrived in Seoul on July 16th. Because Pyongyang was the most severely affected, I went to Pyongyang that night and arrived on the morning of the 17th. I went to various places to inspect and express condolences. I first went to the medical training center to express condolences to the overseas Chinese who were taking refuge. The center accommodated up to 5,000 people at its peak. Except for those who continued to return to China, there were still more than 1,000 people being accommodated as of the 17th. The shelter had facilities such as toilets, bathrooms, infirmaries, thatched sheds, and kitchens. I discussed with Meng Xianxi, the president of the chamber of commerce, to have representatives elected by various groups to go to the hotel in the afternoon to talk to Rongbao. Later, I went to the Provincial Hospital to visit the injured overseas Chinese. There were still about 100 people in the hospital for treatment. Most of them would recover soon and could be discharged from the hospital immediately. In addition, it would take a week or ten days to recover. The general patients were very happy to see Rongbao visit the hospital, and they all said that they were no longer in pain and would recover soon. However, a Mr. Wang was weeping because his wife and children had been killed. He was extremely pitiful. Later, I went to Changshan Cemetery to pay tribute to the dead and injured civilians. The cemetery was divided into five rows. According to the provincial government, 20 people were buried in each row, one coffin and one grave per person. However, there were two infants who were buried together in one coffin. The first row was shorter, and it was said that there were a total of 95 people. Later, I went to inspect the destroyed shops. At 4:00 PM, I met with Meng Xianxi, Wang Zichen, Zhang Jingxian, Xu Weimin, representatives of the Chinese Chamber of Commerce, Wang Zeguo, a representative of the Chinese Restaurant Association, and Liu Wenzhi, a representative of the Chinese Farmers' Association. They said that dozens of injured civilians, women, and children were willing to return to China, and they requested that a way be found to do so. I negotiated with the government officials to prepare a car to send them back to Andong. The overseas Chinese in the shelter were also preparing to leave. Four larger overseas Chinese shops were selected to accommodate them separately. Some overseas Chinese who still lived in the vegetable gardens were returning to farming, and others were returning to their home countries. The Japanese side still agreed to provide food to the unemployed for about ten days. If they were still unable to make a living at that time, the various overseas Chinese chambers of commerce would temporarily provide relief. Rongbao also launched an emergency relief effort for the distressed overseas Chinese in Korea while in the East. More than 10,000 yuan in national currency has been donated by Osaka, Kobe, and other places, and fundraising is still continuing in various places. It will be remitted to Korea one after another. At the same time, Japanese and Korean groups have also sent慰問現金慰問物品 as gifts. Because they were for relief purposes, they were all received and distributed. Later, Zhennampo Consul Xu Sui reported to the Japanese police chief that after investigating Pyongyang overseas Chinese, 108 people died, 3 in Hanchuan, and 1 in Shenghuli. (To be continued)

Yan Xishan Chanting Sutras and Reciting Buddhist Scriptures

Ge Liu Bao All Visit Yan in Wutai

A dispatch from Taiyuan states that Ge Jingen and Liu Guang came to Taiyuan a few days ago to discuss important political affairs in Shanxi Province with Xu Yongchang. On the 20th, Ge Liu and Xu Yongchang's secretary Wang Ping and others took two cars and departed from Taiyuan at about 6:00 PM to visit Yan Xishan in Wutai. When they arrived near Liulin Village in Cao County, the car Ge was riding in suddenly crashed into a tree, causing Ge to suffer a minor arm injury and the engine to be destroyed. Ge Liu and others then shared a car and arrived at Xihui Village in Wutai at about 10:00 PM. Feng Yuxiang lived in this village last year, and Yan is also living here now. Yan's father still lives in his original residence in Hebian Village.

The courtyard where Yan lives is extremely simple, with only a few police and soldiers guarding the perimeter. After Ge Liu and others got out of the car, Yan personally greeted them outside the door and led them to the inner room for a conversation. Yan's attitude was extremely calm. According to what he told Ge Liu, his return to his hometown was purely to visit his relatives and had no political intentions whatsoever. He would not make any comments on the current situation. Apart from living with his family and occasionally visiting the countryside, he did not want to ask about anything else. He declined all visits from friends from all sides, except for those who came for private talks, to avoid suspicion. Ge Liu talked with Yan for about three or four hours before leaving and returning to Taiyuan. However, Ge Liu's meeting with Yan was purely a private matter, and they offered some advice, hoping that Yan would leave Shanxi as soon as possible to quell the rumors. Yan expressed his agreement with the words of the two men.

According to those around Yan, Yan goes to a temple near Xihui Village every day to chant sutras once, to purify his mind and rest. His attitude is extremely silent. Judging by his appearance, he seems to want to sever ties with the world and transcend to a celestial realm. Bao Wenxue, who came with Ge Jingen, also went to Xihui on the morning of the 21st together with Artillery Supervisor Zhou Dai to visit Yan. They are scheduled to return to Taiyuan last night and take the express train to Pingjin with Ge Liu and Xu Yongchang this afternoon. Also, Wang Jingguo and Li Shengda are planning to go to Pingjin with Ge and others to visit Zhang Xueliang, because they failed to meet him on their previous trip to Pingjin as Zhang Xueliang was sick. (22nd)

Chen Cheng Uses Military Fire to Attack the Red Bandits

More Than 2,000 Remnant Guns Recovered

More Than 5,000 Bandits Burned to Death

More Than 5,000 Also Surrendered After Coming Down the Mountain

A dispatch from Nanchang states that the Red Bandits, who gather and disperse unpredictably and whose whereabouts are erratic, often hide in deep mountains and remote valleys, making it impossible to find out their exact location. When the troops of Chen Cheng and Luo Zhuoying recently advanced to suppress the area under Ningdu Xingguo, the bandits hid deep in the local mountains, and the officers and soldiers could do nothing about it. On the 18th and 19th of this month, the southeast wind was strong. Commander Chen then used the strategy of burning the Red Cliffs to order his subordinates to prepare flammables, and at the same time, ambushed heavy troops at the key passes of various mountain passes. At 1:00 PM on the 18th, all the officers and soldiers set fire to the mountains at the same time. At that time, the wind was very strong, and in a short while, the fire had spread all over the mountains and reached the top of the mountains. Many of the bandits' guns, ammunition, and gunpowder exploded due to the fire, and the sound shook the mountains and valleys. Countless bandits were burned to death, and those who dared to rush out through the fire were all annihilated by the ambushing troops guarding the mountain passes. By the 19th, the fire had finally been extinguished. The various units went up the mountain to search and recovered more than 2,000 remnant guns. They found the charred corpses of bandits, about 5,000 or more, scattered all over the ground, and the stench was unbearable. After the Red Bandits in the mountain were eliminated, it was heard that the Red Bandits in other mountains, because the source of food and supplies had been cut off, such as salt and rice, etc., could not be found, and many of them disguised themselves as farmers and came down the mountain to surrender. The Headquarters issued a message that, according to the telegrams from various generals, the number of bandits surrendering in the past five days has been increasing day by day. It is estimated that Sun Lianzhong's troops have taken in more than 800 people in the Gulonggang area, Chen Cheng's and Cai Tingkai's troops have each taken in more than 600 people, Zhao Guantao's and Wei Lihuang's troops have each taken in more than 300 people, Gong Bingfan's troops have taken in more than 900 people, Ma Kun has taken in more than 200 people in Ganzhou, Mao Bingwen has taken in more than 100 people, Shangguan Yunxiang has taken in more than 500 people, and Jiang Dingwen has taken in more than 100 people, totaling more than 5,000 people. Commander-in-Chief Jiang telegraphed the above units, approving them to be temporarily detained, but it is necessary to pay attention to whether they are feigning surrender, and to supervise and persuade them at any time. As for the pseudo-third and fourth armies belonging to Zhu Mao, they have recently fled back from Ningdu Guangchang to Ruijin and are looting money and rice in the western countryside of Ruijin before fleeing into the mountains. Also, because there were too many casualties in the battles of Huangpi Xiaopu Longgang Liantang, etc., it was impossible to replenish them. Whenever a man was encountered, he was captured to fill the bandit army, and women were divided into washing and comforting teams according to their age. Therefore, most of the local people, except for those who have already fled, have been forcibly incorporated into the Red Bandits. The fields are barren, the houses are in ruins, and the scene is extremely tragic. (August 21)

Shandong Province Sends Telegram to Beijing Requesting Relief for Disaster Areas

Twenty-One Counties Report Disasters

A dispatch from Jinan states that the water disasters in Shandong Province have been reported by various counties. The Department of Construction received another telegram yesterday from Song Longming, the district chief of the fifth district of Yi County, stating that the area under his jurisdiction is located in the lower reaches of the Grand Canal in Yi County, and the terrain is the lowest. Since late July, there has been continuous rain, and there have been two floods. The Gushao Xinhe, Jinhefang, Xiawang, Shangwang, and other communities in this district have been submerged in beans and rice by one-third. Unexpectedly, on the 2nd of this month, there was thunder, lightning, and torrential rain that lasted for five days and nights. Mountain floods broke out, and the river rose and the dikes collapsed. The streets of Taizhuang were several feet deep in water. The communities on the banks of the river were all turned into swamps. Su Huanzhang, the chief of the Taizhuang Public Security Bureau, Yuan Guangchang, the chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, and several community leaders took a boat to survey the area. Most of the more than 230 villages under the jurisdiction of this district were submerged in water. Houses collapsed, beans and rice were washed away, people and livestock were drowned, and corpses floated with the water. The residents, old and young, in Taizhuang were standing in the water, and the sight of their wailing was unbearable to witness. This flood is unprecedented in the past thirty years. Please find a way to provide relief to help the disaster victims and save the lives of the people. After receiving the report, the Department of Construction immediately telegraphed the National Government Relief Administration and the Provincial Relief Administration, requesting that relief be provided.

The tail dike of the lower reaches of the Yellow River in Lijin County was breached due to the sudden rise of the river a few days ago. Yue Guangnai, a representative of the disaster area, presented a request to the Department of Civil Affairs and Finance and the River Affairs Bureau for relief. However, since then, although the water level in various streams has dropped, the water level at the breach of the newly built tail dike is still rising sharply. The fields and crops have been flooded, and countless people and livestock have died. The fields and villages in the Northeast Dongxin area have been completely submerged, and the disaster is extremely severe and unprecedented. Yue Guangnai, the disaster area representative of the county, telegraphed the provincial government and the Department of Civil Affairs and Finance and the River Affairs Bureau again on the 24th, requesting immediate relief to save the disaster victims. At the same time, he also telegraphed various agencies, groups, and charities, calling for relief.

The Shandong Provincial Relief Association had previously telegraphed the Central Relief Committee to request relief for the water disasters in Jinxiang and other thirteen counties. Yesterday, because nine counties including Teng Yi had successively reported water disasters, they telegraphed the Central Relief Committee again to request relief. The telegram said: Nanjing Relief Committee, please note. The water disasters in Shandong Province, including Jinxiang and other thirteen counties, have been stated in the telegram on the [omitted] day. Since then, there has been intermittent rain, and the river has overflowed. As of today, nine more counties, including Teng County, Yi County, Ziyang, Dongping, Zhangqiu, Cao County, Yucheng, Wenshang, and Jining, have reported water disasters. Either because of accumulated water causing trouble, or because of mountain floods breaking out, people and livestock have drowned, and houses have collapsed. The remaining old and young are sheltering on high ground, enduring hunger and waiting for assistance. Moreover, the water level of the Yellow River has not stopped rising, which is worrying everywhere. Thinking about the future, it is even more frightening. In addition to distributing the existing funds to provide relief to the most deserving, we hereby present the counties that have successively reported water disasters to you for your kind attention. We beg you to quickly allocate large sums of money to urgently save the remaining lives. We await your orders with utmost urgency. Shandong Provincial Relief Association respectfully.

Suburb of Beijing

Sand Island Embankment Breached for Several Tens of Zhang

Over 70,000 Mu of Farmland Flooded, Over 30,000 People Affected. From Beijing News: Sand Island Embankment, near the outskirts of Beijing, is the primary embankment of Jiangning County. Since the beginning of summer, there have been continuous torrential rains for many days, and both the river tide and river water have risen. Leng Jun, the County Magistrate of Jiangning County, in order to prevent the collapse of the embankment, organized a levee patrol team, appointing Deng Biaoyu, the Captain of the County Police Brigade, as the team leader, and supervised the embankment residents to rush to rescue. Therefore, although there were several dangers, they were fortunately avoided due to effective rescue efforts. However, on the 25th, a sudden hurricane occurred, and the river tide surged more than a foot. That night, the river waves vibrated violently, and the embankment was in extreme danger. Although the levee patrol team rescued all night, by twelve o'clock at night, a section of Mojiawan and a section of the three-hundred-zhang new embankment suddenly collapsed for several tens of zhang, and the rescue was ineffective, resulting in the breach. The County Magistrate of Jiangning County learned of this in the morning and immediately led the heads of the Public Security Bureau, Land Bureau, and Construction Bureau to rush to the site to investigate and plan rescue measures. Sand Island Embankment is the most important embankment in Jiangning County, and its relation is significant. After the breach, the entire embankment area was submerged. It is estimated that there are more than 70,000 mu of embankment farmland, and more than 30,000 people affected by the disaster, which is truly an unprecedented catastrophe. Relief efforts are currently underway.

Fuzhou Business Tax Embezzlement Case

Surveillance Placed on Zheng Jinqing and Four Others

Fuzhou Correspondence: Since Fujian Province changed the various consumption taxes to business taxes, Zheng Jinqing has been in charge of the bamboo paper business tax. However, the original amount was 240,000 yuan per year, but Zheng only acknowledged 150,000 yuan. After the tax was levied, the actual receipts in June and July were 50,000 yuan, but Zheng only remitted 7,000 yuan. This was noticed by Su Wenbing, a staff member of the Business Tax Bureau, who reported it to He Gonggan, the Director of the Department of Finance. He immediately dispatched staff from the Department to the Zhuzhi Bamboo Paper Business Tax Collection Office on August 11 to search, and indeed found many pieces of evidence of embezzlement, and implicated Zhang Zhedan, the Acting Director of the Business Tax Bureau, and Sa Jiaheng, a staff member. The Department of Finance immediately dismissed Zheng Jinqing and appointed Lin Yi to take over, increasing the annual tax quota to 192,000 yuan. However, Xu Xida was willing to take over at 240,000 yuan per year, but was not approved, so he filed a complaint with the provincial government. Yang Shuzhuang, the Chairman, believed that the case was complex and should be thoroughly investigated, and public opinion was also extremely indignant. Therefore, at the meeting of the Provincial Government Committee on August 21, He Gonggan voluntarily submitted a report and requested a review. After deliberation, it was decided to send He Gonggan and Cheng Shiwei to investigate, and then determine a method after the report was submitted. After the meeting, the Provincial Government sent Secretary Wu Xianren, Chief Clerk Lan Dakeng, the Department of Finance sent Section Chief Wang Ziyi and Clerk Chen Yiwei, and the Department of Education sent Section Chief Zheng Qinde and Clerk Cai Shangmo, leading detectives from the Public Security Bureau, taking cars, to Zheng Jinqing, Zhang Zhedan, Sa Jiaheng, and the home of Lin Zhao, the director of the Zhuzhi Bamboo Paper Tax Collection Office, to search. The search started at 1:00 PM and ended at 5:00 PM, but no evidence was found. However, the Provincial Government is determined to thoroughly investigate this case, and strive to get to the bottom of it. Surveillance has already been placed on Zheng Jinqing and four others, and the Minhou Local Court also sent Prosecutor Yang Chongshi to the Business Tax Bureau on the 20th to review the case files and take notes of the answers and confessions of Zhang Zhedan and Zheng Jinqing, in preparation for prosecution. Currently, all parties are paying close attention to this case. More reports about changes will be provided (August 22).

Guangdong Ferry Bombed Again by Bandits

Incident Location: Guangzhou City

Guangzhou Correspondence: The Guangdong Province ferry bombing case has occurred many times in the past month. Recently, another tragic bombing incident occurred in the provincial capital, a place heavily guarded by military police. It was found that the Guangdong Li ferry, which travels between the provincial capital and Chencun, usually anchors along the embankment. At the beginning of this month, it suddenly received a letter from the famous bandit gang Jian Kun, in the name of the Democratic Party, extorting a fee of 2,000 yuan at a time, and a daily bribe of 30 yuan, which must be sent on time, otherwise it would be treated with extreme measures. After receiving the letter, the ferry thought it was just a bandit's intimidation tactic, which was commonplace, and put the letter aside, only taking precautions from time to time. The bandit gang was greatly angered by this. At 7:25 AM on the 20th of this month, as the ferry was about to depart from the province, bandits disguised as passengers boarded the ship, and secretly placed a bomb hidden in a package at the ferry head, mixed in with the crowd and escaped. Later, merchant guilds sent goods, and the goods were stacked on the ship. A ship worker named Zhang Hong noticed a small iron box on the bow of the ship, containing iron hairpins and covered with a straw mat. He felt strange, stepped forward to lift it, thinking it was lost by a passenger, but thinking that it was obstructing traffic, he moved it. As soon as his hand touched the iron box, there was a loud noise, the explosives detonated, and black smoke filled the air. The ferry passengers were shocked and rushed forward to inspect. They saw Zhang Hong lying down injured, his hand blown away, his arm flesh torn off, and blood stains all around him. They knew he had been hit by the bomb and blown up. They immediately asked someone to carry the injured man to the nearby Second Hospital of Zhongda for treatment, cut off traffic, and searched for the bandits, but the bandits had already fled far away and could not be captured. The police officers found several business cards of the bandit gang (signed "Guangdong Provincial People's Party, Dwarf Kun of Panyu") and the iron shell of a bomb on the ship, and sent them to the Haizhu Police Branch for filing. It is reported that Zhang Hong, who was injured, was in serious condition after being admitted to the hospital, and his life may be in danger. When the authorities received the news, they immediately stepped up the arrest of bandits to protect navigation and merchants.

Songjiang

Corpses Discovered for Consecutive Days. Yesterday, amidst the howling of a hurricane, a floating corpse was found beached in the Caihua Jing River outside the west gate. The body was wearing a summer cloth long gown and appeared to be around thirty years old. The local town police reported to the county court prosecutor's office for inspection. The inspection confirmed that the person had died by drowning in the river. A corpse certificate was filled out, and a letter was found in the deceased's possession. The letter was signed Zhang Yuanchang, from Kunshan, stating that he was driven to this by poverty and illness. He hoped that a charitable organization would provide a coffin for burial. The judge instructed the town police to collect the body. Unexpectedly, today (the 27th), another monk's body was found in the Caibi Bridge River outside the west gate. It was later identified as Dahe, a monk from the Great Temple who had moved from the Xilin Temple. He had accumulated 100 yuan, which he lent to Lanfeng, the abbot of the Great Temple. Now, because the monk wanted to move back to the Xilin Temple, he was asking Lanfeng for the money. It is unknown why he suddenly died today. The case has been reported for inspection.

Hubei Refugees Passing Through Due to the flooding in Hubei, many affected people are seeking a livelihood elsewhere. Fengxian

A Unique Divorce and Marriage Case A-Si, the son of Tang Heshang of Taiping Bridge in Sanguantang County, married a girl named A-Jian from the Gao family when he was young. After three years of marriage, they had no children. Recently, due to family matters, a dispute suddenly broke out, and the relationship between the couple deteriorated. Not only did Tang Zi insist on divorce, but the woman also wanted to separate. However, Tang's father felt that it was difficult because his daughter-in-law was diligent in housework and needed assistance in everything. He had a strange idea. The other day, he invited relatives and friends to discuss a solution. He married his son to a woman named Wu, and regarded his daughter-in-law as a goddaughter. He recruited her old relative Wu Hedi as a son-in-law by living in his family. Both parties agreed, and the marriage was completed the other day. This is a rare and interesting story in divorce cases.

Flowers and Rice Damaged by Strong Winds and Rain In this county, since the other day (the 25th), the sky suddenly became cloudy, and strong winds and rain suddenly occurred, lasting for two days and nights without ceasing, resulting in the destruction of flowers and rice and damage to agricultural affairs. Changshu

Public Security Bureau Staff Accused of Accepting Bribes Xiao Gengsheng, who runs a cigarette shop in Junziju Alley outside the south gate of this county, was discovered by the Public Security Bureau. The other day, Inspector Huang was dispatched to crack down. Xiao and others were arrested. However, at that time, it was rumored outside the south gate that the Xiao family had 600 yuan in silver, which was also taken away. The next day, the incident was recorded in the Qinbao newspaper. After seeing the newspaper, Public Security Bureau Director Yin ordered Inspector Lv Baozhong to investigate and reply, but the reply was vague. Unexpectedly, on the morning of the 26th, the Xiao family was arrested again by the Public Security Bureau. At that time, in addition to the cigarette owner Xiao Gengsheng, his old mother and cigarette guest Lu Yinbao and others were also arrested. They were immediately sent to the county. Shen, the judge, opened the court for trial. Xiao Gengsheng admitted that he smoked cigarettes and did not open a cigarette shop. Judge Shen sentenced him to a fine of 200 yuan and imprisonment for one year and one month. His mother was also sentenced to imprisonment for one year and one month and a fine of 80 yuan. Xiao's wife was also in the audience, and after hearing the verdict of her husband, she fell to the ground and fainted. Xiao Gengsheng himself cried and knelt on the ground, begging the judge to redress his grievances. Only then did he admit that he opened a cigarette shop, saying, "I pay more than 100 yuan in bribes every month, and I still have to suffer like this." After hearing this, the judge asked Xiao, "Who do you give your bribes to?" Xiao said, "Everyone in the Public Security Bureau, from the section chief to the patrol officers, receives them." Judge Shen asked if there was any evidence. He replied that there was a notebook to rely on, but he did not bring it and it was hidden at home. He immediately ordered two bailiffs, Zhang Danru and others, to accompany him to retrieve it and submit it to the court. The above-mentioned situation was indeed found. Xiao and others were detained for investigation. At that time, the Public Security Bureau was shocked when it heard the news. Director Yin and others went to see County Magistrate Tan and first detained the patrol officer Lu Zhenying who had handled the case, and the rest were thoroughly investigated.

Wuxi

Zhu, Who Conspired to Harm Her Husband, Was Sent to the Court for Trial Zhou Jiashan, Director of the Eighth Branch of the Public Security Bureau, received a letter from Li Boru and others, the head of the Gengdu Township in the Third District, stating that the farmer Lu A-mei was old and weak, and his wife Zhu had an affair with Jiang A-xue, a farmhand from Changshu. A-mei slightly interfered, and A-xue and Zhu used beatings and threats. Recently, they have intensified their efforts. A-xue said to A-mei that he had to be strangled with a rope. The next day, A-mei found a hemp rope next to his wife's pillow, measuring one zhang and seven feet long. A-mei was so frightened that he ran out and has not returned for three days. After receiving the report, Director Zhou immediately ordered the police to summon Lu Zhu and Jiang A-xue to the case. After a preliminary trial, they were sent to the County Public Security Bureau and then to the County Court for trial in accordance with the law.

Appeal to Issue Silk Industry Public Bonds The Silk Factory Industry Union of this county found that the Silk Industry Relief Public Bond Regulations have been promulgated for more than a month, but have not been issued. Yesterday, they sent a telegram to Minister Kong of the Ministry of Industry and Minister Song of the Ministry of Finance in Nanjing, asking them to have mercy on the suffering of unemployed workers and quickly change the procedures and issue them immediately to maintain the silk industry and comfort the public.

Reorganization of the Jiangsu Provincial Business Tax Bureau Since the beginning of this year, the Jiangsu Provincial Business Tax Bureau has established bureaus in various counties to handle various procedures such as investigation and registration, and the chambers of commerce have assisted in the business. Most of the industries have separately acknowledged the entire amount. The collection began on April 1. Now the first quarter's taxes have been successively paid separately. However, after several months, the collection has not been smooth. The taxes reported by the counties to the Department of Finance are only about 100,000 yuan, and the various expenses after the establishment of the bureaus have reached 70,000 to 80,000 yuan in the past six months. Moreover, merchants in various counties mostly insist that the starting date of the tax should be from June. In order to promote the new tax and achieve the greatest benefit, it is necessary to rectify it. After thorough consultation between Director Xu of the Department of Finance and Chairman Ye, it was decided to reorganize on September 1. Except for Zhenjiang, Suzhou, Wuxi and other 18 counties, which will set up separate bureaus, the business tax bureaus in the remaining counties will be attached to the finance bureaus, and the director of the bureau will be concurrently held by the director of the finance bureau. For small counties without a finance bureau, the county magistrate will concurrently hold the position in order to save expenses. Moreover, the Suzhou area is vast and the commercial markets are densely packed, ranking first among the counties in Jiangsu Province. At this time of active rectification, it is impossible to handle without smart and capable people. Yang Wubian, the director of the Wuxi Business Tax Bureau, is extremely capable, and after the tax was levied, he was able to maintain order, and his achievements were the best among the counties. It has now been decided to transfer him to Suzhou, and Wang Shutang, the former director of Suzhou, will be transferred to Wuxi. The appointment has been issued. Director Yang has rushed to handle the handover procedures and went to Zhenjiang to meet with Director Xu of the Department of Finance to ask for instructions on everything. The Wuxi County Chamber of Commerce believed that Director Yang was able to understand the difficulties of merchants in Wuxi and especially sent a telegram to Director Xu, requesting that he be exempted from the transfer in order to keep a skilled person.

Lin Huanbin, a Famous Bandit from Yixing, Surrenders Himself with Weapons Lin Huanbin, a famous bandit from Yixing, is from Kaosi Township, Huzhen. He has three brothers, all of whom are farmers. Last year, Huanbin went out to mill rice and joined the bandit party, lurking in the mountains. He went to Guangde the month before. Recently, the Yixing County Government has repeatedly received reports that Lin Huanbin participated in various robbery cases and ordered Lu Maohe, the head of the sixth district, to arrest Huanbin's brother Guangwen. Huanbin heard the news and thought that he was the only one who was a bandit and should not implicate his brothers. He immediately took a letter stating his willingness to reform, a wooden-cased gun, and twenty-five bullets and surrendered himself to the Water Police Inspection Office stationed in the town. The inspector Bai Guosheng immediately telegraphed the Ninth Team Headquarters and dispatched Sun Meizhang, the patrol officer of Patrol Boat No. 2, and Ye Songqi, the patrol officer of Patrol Boat No. 8, to inquire. When the boat arrived at the Danjia Alley in Huli Xu, Inspector Bai and the surrendered bandit Lin Huanbin were already waiting in the mulberry field. They were immediately taken aboard the patrol boat. Just as they were about to leave, Lu Maohe, the head of the Sixth District, rushed to the patrol boat and took Lin to the district office and convened the town's defense regiment. Together with the water police, they ordered Lin to lead them to the mountains to arrest the remaining bandits, but they had already fled and nothing was gained. Officer Sun and others then escorted Bandit Lin back to the team headquarters. After interrogation by Captain Huang Cheng, they sent the police to escort Bandit Lin to Xixi and return to the district headquarters for trial. It is reported that Lin Huanbin claimed to be the beloved disciple of Tang Jinbiao, a famous bandit leader. After Tang fled, Lin supervised his subordinates, who were extremely fierce. Now, due to internal disagreements and the vigorous pursuit by the government, he is willing to reform.

Zhenjiang

Reports of Disasters in Various Townships Amidst Strong Winds and Rain. Since the continuous rain in Zhenjiang last month, the river tide has been rising, and the Jinshan Road area near the river has become a swamp, and residents are complaining. Last night, the weather suddenly changed, with strong winds and heavy rain. The houses along the riverbank completely collapsed and were washed away. The areas along the river in the first district suffered the most, and telegrams reported the disasters. The details are as follows: (1) Jiuli Township: Due to strong winds and heavy rain last night at 2:00, the river tide rose above the riverbank, causing more than 2,000 mu of farmland from Ganlu Temple to Xiangshan to be flooded, and 40 to 50 houses were washed down. Debris floated in the water, and everything was washed away. The victims climbed trees and mountains and cried out in various ways. The water inside the levee was more than a zhang deep, and shallow areas were four or five feet deep. The river tide was overflowing, and there was no end in sight. The victims had nowhere to stay. (2) Baojin Township: The township, east from Ganlu Temple to the boundary of Dengxian, has a total of two to three hundred mu of fields, all completely submerged by water. The water depth is about five or six feet. Dozens of wood sheds and more than a hundred households were all submerged in water. (3) Dingye Township: The township is connected to Huangni Township. Due to the collapse of the riverbank in Huangni Township, the crops had been affected. The accumulated water has not yet receded, and they are still working hard to rush to rescue. Suddenly, heavy rain caused the river tide to overflow, completely submerging more than 700 mu of crops, and more than 120 households were submerged in the water. Livestock and debris were washed away. More than 700 victims were either avoiding on the roof or climbing tree branches, desperately calling for help, which is very pitiful. The Rescue Bureau has been requested to send red boats to provide relief. (4) Huangni Township: The township suffered the most damage last month. Yesterday at 4:00 in the morning, due to heavy rain and strong winds, the Longgeng levee collapsed another twenty zhang, and the waves were overwhelming, destroying more than 30 houses. More than a hundred residents on the shore were submerged in water and are in urgent need of relief. The above is the situation of the disaster in various townships along the river in the first district. The disaster in other districts and villages should also be similar to that in the first district. Although the crops in the mountainous areas had a relatively good harvest before, the strong winds last night may have made them sterile. The Zhenjiang County Party Department and the County Government believed that the disasters in various townships were severe and needed relief urgently. They convened various institutions and groups to organize a disaster relief committee to prepare to raise donations and distribute them. Now that the disaster in various townships has worsened, and the victims in various townships along the river are waiting for food, the relief cannot be delayed any longer. A meeting has been scheduled at 2:00 PM on the 29th in the Chamber of Commerce to jointly discuss the method of distributing emergency relief.

Proposed Financial Remedies: Anhui Province's financial income is insufficient to cover its expenditures. According to reports from the authorities, the deficit for the 20th year of the Republic has reached 1.5 million yuan. Combined with the arrears from the 19th year, the total deficit is 2 million yuan. Currently, the province is experiencing severe floods, exacerbating the deficit. The Finance Department is proposing two remedial measures: one is to levy an export tax on rice, and the other is to divert funds from road construction bonds. There are also plans to raise funds through surcharges on tobacco and alcohol, and to issue 3 million yuan in public bonds. These plans are being submitted to the Central Government for approval. It is also planned that after the 3 million yuan public bonds are issued, the funds from the road construction bonds will be returned.

Various Relief Efforts Amidst the Chaos: The flood situation in Anhui Province is extremely severe. The Relief Committee has agreed to allocate 170,000 yuan in relief funds and has dispatched the committee's secretary, Hong Jiong, to Anhui for inspection. Du Yuesheng of Shanghai generously donated 1,200 bags of flour, sending his representative, Jiang Zuozhou, to Anhui for distribution. Ma Jidi, an Anhui native in Beijing, donated 5,000 yuan to the Luning County Flood Relief Association for distribution. The Anqing Chinese Medicine Association has formed a flood relief clinic team, which opened on the 23rd near Guangjiwei. The Zhejiang Provincial Government has provided 3,000 yuan in aid to Anhui.

Page 13

Local News

Song Ziwen Speaks

Relief Bonds for Flood Victims

Primarily to Issue 10 Million Yuan First

Entrust to Existing Fund Committee for Management

Minister Song made the following statement yesterday regarding the issuance of relief bonds for flood victims:

To provide relief for the current floods, the government originally planned to issue 10 million yuan in public bonds. This is a preliminary measure, as the exact amount of funds needed for relief will be determined after a detailed investigation and study by the Flood Relief Committee. The Legislative Yuan is currently advocating for the issuance of 80 million yuan in public bonds and proposes to use a portion of it to purchase relief grain. This seems to overlook the government's ongoing negotiations with the U.S. government to purchase American wheat. Regarding the establishment of a separate fund management committee, while the existing fund management committee has maintained the credit of public bonds with considerable success, it seems to have been disregarded. I am now proposing to the Central Government that, while the purchase of American wheat is under negotiation and the committee's proposal is being prepared, the original plan to issue 10 million yuan in public bonds should be implemented first, and the existing fund management committee should be entrusted with its management. It is well known that the current flood relief requires a large amount of funds. I fully support the government's efforts to raise funds for disaster relief to the best of its financial ability. However, we must be practical in addressing this issue. Therefore, as a first step in terms of finance, we should still approve the issuance of 10 million yuan in flood relief bonds according to the original proposal.

Yesterday Morning

Zhu Qinglan and Others Fly to Hankou

Departing while Telegraphing Shandong Province for Aid

Zhu Qinglan of the National Flood Relief Committee, accompanied by Cha Liangzhao, a member of the North China Charitable Relief Association, and Zhang Yuanshan, the director of the Shanghai Chinese and Foreign Relief Association, took China Aviation Corporation's seaplane No. 15 from Longhua Airport at 7:00 a.m. yesterday to Hankou to investigate the flood situation. They arrived in Hankou at 2:10 p.m. yesterday to conduct an on-site investigation in order to formulate emergency relief measures upon their return to Shanghai. It is also reported that Zhu and others are expected to return to Shanghai by the same plane in the next few days to report everything to Song Ziwen, the chairman of the Flood Relief Committee. Before leaving Shanghai, Zhu also telegraphed the Shandong provincial authorities for aid. The telegram reads: "To General Ma Zizhen, Shandong Poison Eradication Association, and various legal entities: The floods along the Yangtze River are disastrous and unprecedented in centuries. When I passed through Jinan a few days ago, I asked Zhou Baipeng to convey to He Chunlao to initiate disaster relief. I am now shocked to learn of Chunlao's passing yesterday. I am deeply saddened. I have always admired your enthusiasm for public welfare and your high reputation in Shandong. I respectfully request that you forward this to Chairman Han and unite with various legal entities to raise funds for relief, thereby expressing sympathy. Shandong is my second hometown. In the past, it suffered repeated disasters, and I was grateful for the generous assistance from various charitable organizations in the North and South. I cannot stand idly by during this flood in Jiangnan. On behalf of millions of flood victims, I bow nine times in advance. Shaojiang, my younger brother, please also convey my condolences. Sincerely, Zhu Qinglan."

At 2:00 p.m. yesterday, various Chinese flood relief organizations in Shanghai held a meeting and resolved to unanimously elect Zhu Qinglan, director of the disaster area working group of the National Flood Relief Committee, to preside over all work related to the disaster areas.

News from All Sectors on Disaster Relief Yesterday

A Large Number of Refugees Arriving in Shanghai Today

A large number of refugees will arrive in Shanghai successively. The issues of accommodation and fundraising are extremely urgent, and all sectors are working hard to prepare. The following is a summary of various news items heard yesterday:

Large Batch of Hankou Flood Victims Arriving in Shanghai Today

The Flood Relief Committee, considering the severity of the flood in Wuhan, has specially requested the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company to send the Jiangong vessel to Hankou to rescue flood victims. According to news from the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company yesterday, the Jiangong vessel is expected to arrive in Shanghai at 1:00 p.m. today.

Ningbo-Shaoxing Emergency Relief Association Establishes Accommodation Centers

The Ningbo-Shaoxing Emergency Relief Association for the Hankou Disaster has dispatched the Xin Ningxing steamer, which was sent to Hankou to assist disaster-stricken fellow villagers. The ship departed from Hankou on the 20th with over 1,000 refugees and is expected to sail directly to Ningbo. However, due to insufficient coal, it may stop in Shanghai tomorrow to replenish coal. The association is deeply concerned that the increasing number of Hankou refugees arriving in Shanghai may disrupt order due to overcrowding. Therefore, it has borrowed the Ding Siming Guild Hall as the first accommodation center, the Yongxitang of the Zhejiang-Shaoxing Guild Hall as the second accommodation center, and the Zhejiang-Ningbo Guild Hall as the third accommodation center. Regarding the situation in Ningbo, County Magistrate Chen Guanling of Yin County is currently in Shanghai and has been contacted. When the Xin Ningxing arrives in Ningbo, additional military police will be dispatched to take care of the refugees and arrange for accommodation and transportation. It is also reported that the association received a telegram from Hankou urgently requesting a large quantity of biscuits for relief. It immediately purchased 60 large boxes, 30 of which were shipped on Saturday, and the remaining boxes are planned to be shipped to Hankou on Monday.

Zhabei Charity Group Prepares Accommodation

Wang Binyan, director of the Zhabei Charity Group, and Supervisor Cai Yuanfu, visited the Sun Temple Congee Kitchen and the Yangzhou Guild Hall yesterday with staff to inspect the buildings and make preparations. They ordered the staff to quickly organize and clean up the premises to accommodate flood victims from various districts arriving in Shanghai.

The Shanghai Banking Association convened a meeting of bank representatives at 4:00 p.m. yesterday to discuss the proposal to raise funds for disaster relief. Over 50 representatives attended. Ye Moxiao was elected as chairman. It was resolved that (1) the Shanghai Money Exchange Association was also holding a meeting that day to discuss the matter. It was proposed to hold a joint meeting with the Money Exchange Association tomorrow to facilitate joint action. The resolution was approved. Executive committee members from both the Banking Association and the Money Exchange Association would attend the joint meeting. (2) The name of the association was decided to be the "Emergency Relief Association for Flood Victims in Various Provinces," jointly established by the Banking Association and the Money Exchange Association. (3) Before the fundraising methods of the Banking Association were finalized, for the sake of urgently rescuing the flood victims, the representatives of each bank present at the meeting were requested to ask their respective banks to raise a total amount, which would be advanced by the banks first. Within three days, the association would be informed, and the funds would be handed over to well-organized relief organizations for rapid distribution. (4) Fundraising would be divided into two categories: bank contributions and employee contributions. Employees could either donate freely or have contributions deducted from their salaries. The specific methods would be determined by each bank. (5) The fundraising target for the banking sector was set at 1 million yuan. The meeting adjourned after the resolutions were passed.

The China Jisheng Society, in light of the unprecedented calamities in various provinces, had no choice but to hold an emergency meeting to address the most pressing needs and rush to provide assistance. The society has allocated an additional 5,000 yuan to meet the urgent needs. However, the society's old relief efforts are not yet completed, and new relief efforts are coming one after another. The old debts have not been paid off, and new debts are huge. The calamity is so tragic that it cannot be ignored, but there is no money to provide relief. It is hoped that philanthropists and benefactors at home and abroad will be able to provide independent relief or join the society to work together to remedy the disaster in the slightest possible way.

Enthusiastic Assistance from All Sectors

Donations from Children and Newspaper Vendors: The Shanghai Fundraising Association for Flood Emergency Relief in Various Provinces received donations from Cui Lutong of Datong, Anhui Province, and Liu Yiming of Shanghai, which are truly commendable. Cui Lutong is also skilled in calligraphy and has strong brushwork and is willing to write 50 pairs of couplets to be sent to Shanghai for sale to raise relief funds. The other is a poor newspaper vendor, Liu Yiming. According to his letter to the Emergency Relief Association, "I am a poor man selling newspapers at the Qinglian Pavilion, earning only four or five dimes a day. After expenses, I have only one or two hundred cash left. Sometimes, when business is bad, I have to borrow money at high interest to make ends meet. It is really hard. But compared to the fellow citizens who are suffering from the flood, I am much better off. Therefore, I am sending all the money I earned from selling newspapers for the past three days, including principal and interest, totaling one yuan and four dimes, and 26 copper coins. I have already sent the money to the Emergency Relief Association yesterday, saying, 'Poor people have no money, please accept it and save a life.' As he spoke, he sobbed and wiped away his tears."

Donations from the Faculty and Staff of the Wusong Merchant Marine School: The Wusong Merchant Marine School held a school affairs meeting on the 25th, as the autumn semester was about to begin. Yang first announced that he would donate his entire month's salary (totaling 400 yuan). The remaining faculty and staff decided to donate salaries according to the following methods: those with a monthly salary of 400 yuan or more would donate 30% of their salary, those with a monthly salary of 300 yuan would donate 25%, those with a monthly salary of 200 yuan would donate 20%, those with a monthly salary of 100 yuan would donate 15%, those with a monthly salary of 50 yuan would donate 10%, and those with a monthly salary of less than 50 yuan would donate at least 2 yuan. The resolution was passed and sent to the disaster relief organization for verification and remittance, and a copy was sent to the Ministry for record-keeping.
